province_event = {
    id = autobuild_startbuilding.1 #start ca_bandits_1
    desc = autobuild_startbuilding.1.desc 
    picture = GFX_evt_council 
    is_triggered_only = yes 
    notification = yes 
    immediate = {
        ab_abcf_trigger_repeat = yes 
        IF = {
            limit = { any_province_holding = { has_building = ca_ab_ph_ca_bandits_1}} 
            province_event = { id = autobuild_pay.3}
            trigger_switch = {
                on_trigger = has_province_flag 
                ab_tech_con_level_0 = {
                    province_event = { id = autobuild_finishbuilding.1 days = 7}
                    add_province_modifier = { name = ca__ab_mod_ca_bandits_1 duration = 7}
                    }
                ab_tech_con_level_1 = {
                    province_event = { id = autobuild_finishbuilding.1 days = 6}
                    add_province_modifier = { name = ca__ab_mod_ca_bandits_1 duration = 6}
                    }

                    province_event = { id = autobuild_finishbuilding.1 days = 6}
                    add_province_modifier = { name = ca__ab_mod_ca_bandits_1 duration = 6}
